[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue manifests as a timeout error reported by libFuzzer, which is a [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcoverage-guided fuzzing engine. When libFuzzer reports a timeout, it means that [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeyond the maximum allowed time limit [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtypically configured at several seconds or [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis timeout behavior typically indicates one of several potential performance or [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Algorithmic Complexity Issues**: The code may contain algorithms with poor time[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomplexity [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., exponential or high-polynomial complexity[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that become [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproblematic with certain inputs[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Infinite or Near-Infinite Loops**: Logic errors that cause loops to execute for[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexcessive iterations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Deadlocks or Resource Contention**: In concurrent code, potential deadlock [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msituations or resource blocking[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Denial of Service [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDoS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Vulnerability**: The timeout may represent a [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdenial-of-service condition where specially crafted input can cause the application[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWhile not always a security vulnerability in the traditional sense, timeout [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconditions can represent availability issues that may be exploitable to cause [0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy for libFuzzer Timeout in PDFBox Type1Parser[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe timeout issue stems from **two infinite loop vulnerabilities** in the [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mType1Parser class that occur when processing malformed Adobe Type [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m fonts. These [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerabilities are regressions of previously fixed issues [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPDFBOX-[0m[1;36m5624[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Vulnerable Locations:**[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m217[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m223[0m[39m** in `[0m[1;35mreadEncoding[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvuln_3[0m[1;39m)[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m640[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m644[0m[39m** in `[0m[1;35mparseBinary[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvuln_4[0m[1;39m)[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBoth loops share the same problematic pattern:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekKind[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTokenType[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"expected"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m ⚠️ Return value ignored - no EOF detection[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why This Causes Infinite Loops:**[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- When malformed input reaches EOF without the expected tokens, `[0m[1;35mreadToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreturns null[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mpeekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` becomes null, causing `[0m[1;35mpeekKind[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to return false[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The negated condition `![0m[1;39m([0m[39mfalse && [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` evaluates to true[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Loop continues indefinitely, repeatedly consuming null tokens[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- libFuzzer detects this as a timeout error[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Detailed Fix Implementation[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mApply EOF detection to both vulnerable loops by checking the return value of [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mnextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Fix #[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Type1Parser.java - [0m[1;35mreadEncoding[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m222[0m[1;39m)[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Current vulnerable code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m217[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m223[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:**[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekKind[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.NAME[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        && [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"dup"[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                || [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"readonly"[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                || [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"def"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Fixed code:**[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekKind[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.NAME[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                || [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"readonly"[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                || [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"def"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Should have found dup, readonly or def?! EOF?"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Fix #[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Type1Parser.java - [0m[1;35mparseBinary[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m643[0m[1;39m)[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Current vulnerable code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m640[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m644[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:**[0m                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekKind[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.LITERAL[0m[1;39m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Why This Fix Is Optimal[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Minimal and Targeted:**[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Only modifies the two vulnerable loops [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m4[0m[39m lines of code total[0m[1;39m)[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to lexer, token system, or other parser methods[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Preserves all existing functionality and semantics[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Proven Pattern:**[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Matches the fix pattern from PDFBOX-[0m[1;36m5624[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mprevious similar issue[0m[1;39m)[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Consistent with safe patterns already used elsewhere in Type1Parser [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m556[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m568[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m474[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m479[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m513[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m518[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Converts DoS vulnerability into proper error handling[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Maintains Parser Behavior:**[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Well-formed fonts continue to parse correctly[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Malformed fonts fail fast with clear error messages instead of hanging[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All existing test cases remain valid[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Error messages aid debugging: [0m[32m"Should have found dup, readonly or def?! EOF?"[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclearly indicates the expected tokens[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Security Improvement:**[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Eliminates DoS attack vector from crafted PDFs with malformed Type [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m fonts[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Prevents resource exhaustion in production environments[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Provides immediate feedback rather than silent timeouts[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Implementation Considerations[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No Side Effects:**[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The lexer's `[0m[1;35mnextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method returns the current lookahead token before [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mupdating it[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Checking its return value doesn't affect the parser state[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The IOException thrown is already part of the method signature[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All callers already handle IOException appropriately[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Preserves Lenient Parsing:**[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Type1Parser is designed to be [0m[32m"forgiving"[0m[39m for non-conformant fonts[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This fix doesn't make it stricter - it only prevents infinite loops[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The parser still handles various font format variations as before[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Only truly malformed [0m[1;39m([0m[39mEOF before expected tokens[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m fonts will error[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No Impact on Other Code:**[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Comprehensive analysis confirms only these two loops are vulnerable[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Other token-skipping loops already use safe patterns:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Explicit null checks in loop conditions [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m556[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m564[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Bounded for-loops with EOF checks [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m116[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m148[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m332[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m358[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m581[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m635[0m[1;39m)[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Positive conditions that naturally handle null [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m226[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m234[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - While loops with proper EOF handling [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m474[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m479[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m513[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m518[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Thread Safety:**[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Type1Parser is not thread-safe by design [0m[1;39m([0m[39msingle-use parser instance[0m[1;39m)[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Type1Lexer maintains internal state but is only accessed by one parser[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fix doesn't introduce any concurrency issues[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Verification Strategy[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Existing Test Compatibility:**[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All existing unit tests should pass without modification[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fix only affects error paths [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmalformed input reaching EOF[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Well-formed fonts in test suite will parse identically[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**New Test Cases Needed:**[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Malformed font with incomplete encoding array [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtriggers vuln_3[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Malformed font missing [0m[35m/[0m[95mCharStrings[0m[39m dictionary [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtriggers vuln_4[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Both should throw IOException instead of timeout[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Verify error messages are informative[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Fuzzing Validation:**[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Re-run libFuzzer with the same timeout configuration[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Previously timeout-triggering inputs should now fail with IOException[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fuzzer should continue finding other potential issues without hanging[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Alternative Approaches Considered and Rejected[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Refactor to use safe loop pattern**[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Replace both loops with explicit `Token peekToken = [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; while [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mpeekToken != null && [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` pattern[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Rejected:** More invasive, changes working code unnecessarily, higher risk of [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintroducing bugs[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Add iteration counter with maximum limit**[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Track loop iterations and throw exception after threshold[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Rejected:** Arbitrary limits may break valid but complex fonts, doesn't address[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroot cause[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Modify Type1Lexer to throw exception instead of returning null**[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Change lexer contract to throw EOFException[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Rejected:** Would require changes throughout entire fontbox module, affects [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmany call sites[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Use timeout mechanism in parser**[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add time-based checks within loops[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Rejected:** Performance overhead, platform-dependent, doesn't fix the logic [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39merror[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m. Long-term Recommendations[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Code Quality Improvements:**[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Add static analysis rule to detect `[0m[1;35mnextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` calls without null checks[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Consider standardizing on one safe token consumption pattern[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Document the EOF handling requirements in Type1Lexer javadoc[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Add integration tests with fuzzer-generated malformed inputs to test suite[0m       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m. Summary[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix strategy addresses the libFuzzer timeout by adding EOF detection to two [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecific infinite loops in Type1Parser. The solution is minimal [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[39m null checks[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproven [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmatches previous fixes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and preserves all existing functionality while [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meliminating a DoS vulnerability. The fix converts infinite loops into proper error [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconditions, allowing malformed fonts to fail fast with clear error messages instead[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof causing timeouts.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
